***hakken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hakken.html>hakken</a> (4034)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hacken.html>hacken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hackon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hakkōną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hakken.html>hakken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hack, chop</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:halle.html>halle</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*halla</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hallō</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱel-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hide, cover, conceal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/half-pipe" class="extiw" title="w:half-pipe"><a href = vnd.unilang:half-pipe.html>half-pipe</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/half-pipe" class="extiw" title="w:half-pipe">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/14/Halfpipe_Snowboard.jpg/220px-Halfpipe_Snowboard.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/14/Halfpipe_Snowboard.jpg/330px-Halfpipe_Snowboard.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/14/Halfpipe_Snowboard.jpg/440px-Halfpipe_Snowboard.jpg 2x" data-file-width="500" data-file-height="333" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>A halfpipe used for <a href = vnd.unilang:snowboarding.html>snowboarding</a></div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:half-pipe.html>half-pipe</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">half-pipes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">skateboarding<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:snowboarding.html>snowboarding</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> etc.</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A structure used to perform tricks, approximately semicircular in cross-section, resembling the bottom <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> of a cylinder laying down.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2009</b>,  January 24,  “Randy Starkman”, in  <cite>Silver medal eases pain for Batchelor at world championships</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.thestar.com/Sports/article/576600">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">But the kid who washed <a href = vnd.unilang:windows.html>windows</a> for $2 an hour when he <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> 8 so he could buy his first <a href = vnd.unilang:snowboard.html>snowboard</a> served notice he could be a contender at the 2010 Vancouver Olympics with a silver medal yesterday in <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a>'s <b>halfpipe</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***half.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> (754)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*halbaz</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">halb</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">heal</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">halv</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">with numbers</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> before the next whole
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:tien.html>tien</a></i>
<dl><dd><b><a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a></b> past nine (i.e. <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> of the tenth hour)</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ander.html>ander</a><b><a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a></b></i>
<dl><dd>one and a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> before two, with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ander.html>ander</a></i> originally meaning <i>second</i>)</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li>not completely cooked, <span class="Latn" lang="en">half-baked</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of meat</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">medium <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span></li>
<li>crazy, foolish, <span class="Latn" lang="en">half-baked</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:halfhartig.html>halfhartig</a> (105779)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hart.html>hart</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">heart</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>  + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:halsstarrig.html>halsstarrig</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Halsstarre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">obstinacy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stiff-neckedness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hals.html>hals</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">neck</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">star</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stiff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>

***halt.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:halt.html>halt</a> (3104)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:halte.html>halten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hold; to <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_3">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:halt.html>halt</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention"> | Imperative | singular |  of <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:halte.html>halten</a></i>.</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:halt.html>halt</a>!</strong>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a>!, wait!</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:halt.html>halt</a></i>, pertaining to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">halto</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">soon, fast</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*haldiz</i>, an adverbial comparative like <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*batiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:halt.html>halt</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> modal particle</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Indicating that something <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> generally known, or cannot be changed, or the like; often untranslatable</span>; so, just, simply, indeed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>Er</a> ist <b><a href = vnd.unilang:halt.html>halt</a></b> ein Idiot.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>So</b> he’s an idiot.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Dann müssen wir <b><a href = vnd.unilang:halt.html>halt</a></b> härter arbeiten.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Then <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a>’<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> <b>just</b> have to work <a href = vnd.unilang:harder.html>harder</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> originally southern German and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> still so considered by some contemporary dictionaries. It <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a>, however, become common throughout the language area during the past decades.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_3">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="de">eben</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:halt.html>halt</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>
<ol><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> ~ toeroepen</i>: <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stilstand.html>stilstand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brengen.html>brengen</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mogelijk.html>mogelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beweging.html>beweging</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:halt.html>halt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:roepen.html>roepen</a>?</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>

***halter.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:halter.html>halter</a> (31869)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:halter.html>halter</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">helter</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">helfter</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hælfter</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hælftre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:halter.html>halter</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*halftrō</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*halftrijaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">harness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)KelH-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">half-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-ter</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">helter</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:halter.html>halter</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low </p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:halter.html>halter</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:halters.html>halters</a></b>)
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2b/Halter_%28PSF%29.png/220px-Halter_%28PSF%29.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="237" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2b/Halter_%28PSF%29.png/330px-Halter_%28PSF%29.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2b/Halter_%28PSF%29.png/440px-Halter_%28PSF%29.png 2x" data-file-width="1805" data-file-height="1943" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:halter.html>Halter</a> that are placed <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the horse head</div></div></div>
<ol><li>A bitless headpiece of rope or straps, placed on the head of animals such as cattle or <a href = vnd.unilang:horses.html>horses</a> to lead or tie them.</li>
<li>A rope with a <a href = vnd.unilang:noose.html>noose</a>, for hanging criminals; the gallows rope.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1603</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michel_de_Montaigne" class="extiw" title="w:Michel de Montaigne"><a href = vnd.unilang:michel.html>Michel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:montaigne.html>Montaigne</a></a>,  chapter 12, in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Florio" class="extiw" title="w:John Florio">John Florio</a>, transl., <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Essays_(Montaigne)" class="extiw" title="w:Essays (Montaigne)">The Essayes,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="or, Morall, Politike and Millitarie Discourses of Lo. Michaell de Montaigne, Knight of the Noble Order of St. Michaell, and One of the Gentlemen in Ordinary of the French King, Henry the Third His Chamber">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a></cite>, book II, printed at London |  By <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Valentine_Simmes" class="extiw" title="w:Valentine Simmes"><a href = vnd.unilang:val.html>Val</a>[entine] Simmes</a> for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Edward Blount</a><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="dwelling in Paules churchyard">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/946730821">946730821</a></small>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">And <i>Crates</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a>, that love <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> cured with hunger, if not by time; and in him that liked not these two meanes, by the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:halter.html>halter</a></b> <span style="font-size:85%;">[transl. <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:hart.html>hart</a></i>]</span>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1913</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Barr_(writer)" class="extiw" title="w:Robert Barr (writer)">Robert Barr</a>,  chapter 4, in  <cite><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL1796924W">Lord Stranleigh Abroad</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">“<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>No rogue e’<a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> felt the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:halter.html>halter</a></b> draw, with a good opinion of the law, and perhaps my own detestation of the law arises from my having frequently broken it.<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>.”</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:halter.html>halter</a> top.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ham.html>ham</a> (4595)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_7">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hamme</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hammō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kónh₂m</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_8">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ham.html>ham</a></span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">cured pork from the thigh of a swine</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***hamlet.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hamlet.html>hamlet</a> (8399)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:hamlet.html>hamlet</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">hamelet</i>, a borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">hamelet</i>, diminutive of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">hamel</i> (Modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">hameau</i>), in turn diminutive of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:ham.html>ham</a></i>, of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Germanic languages">Germanic</a></span> origin. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">home</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">heem</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Heim</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hām</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hamlet.html>hamlet</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hamlets.html>hamlets</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A small village or a group of <a href = vnd.unilang:houses.html>houses</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A village that does not have its own church.</li>
<li>Any of the fish of the genus <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Hypoplectrus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Hypoplectrus"><i>Hypoplectrus</i></a></span> in the family Serranidae.</li></ol>
</body>

***hamm.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hamm.html>hamm</a> (60779)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hammō</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hamme</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ham.html>ham</a></i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">hamma</i> (dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:hamm.html>Hamm</a></i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hǫm</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latinx headword" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:hamm.html>hamm</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:ham.html>ham</a>, inner knee</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hammaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs"><a href = vnd.unilang:ham.html>ham</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">hamme</i> (Low <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:hamm.html>Hamm</a></i>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latinx headword" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:hamm.html>hamm</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>enclosure, piece of enclosed <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a></li></ol>
</body>

***hamsteren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hamsteren.html>hamsteren</a> (64847)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>1916 or 1917. Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">hamstern</i>, inspired by the way <a href = vnd.unilang:hamsters.html>hamsters</a> use their cheek pouches to keep food for <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> use. Older dictionaries tend to stress the secrecy or illegality of the act. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hamster.html>hamster</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hamsteren.html>hamsteren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hoard <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">e.g. food, supplies</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, typically for emergencies
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Italianen <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hamsteren.html>hamsteren</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:pasta.html>pasta</a>, Nederlanders <a href = vnd.unilang:wiet.html>wiet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:amerikanen.html>Amerikanen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:machinegeweren.html>machinegeweren</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Italians <b>hoard</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:pasta.html>pasta</a>, Dutch people [hoard] weed and Americans [hoard] machine <a href = vnd.unilang:guns.html>guns</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:winkel.html>winkel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a> <b>hamsterende</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:bejaarden.html>bejaarden</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The shop <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> full of <b>hoarding</b> elderly people.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hamsteren.html>hamsteren</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:overgankelijk.html>overgankelijk</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorraad.html>voorraad</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanleggen.html>aanleggen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> voedselschaarste
<dl><dd><ul><li><i> <a href = vnd.unilang:koffie.html>Koffie</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hamsteren.html>hamsteren</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:omdat.html>omdat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:prijs.html>prijs</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stijgen.html>stijgen</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> hamstring (17122)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***hamvraag.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hamvraag.html>hamvraag</a> (33331)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ham.html>ham</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:ham.html>ham</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vraag.html>vraag</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">question</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The term originated from the 1950s Dutch radio quiz <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nl:Mastklimmen_(radioprogramma)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:nl:Mastklimmen (radioprogramma)">Mastklimmen</a>, in which contestants received a <a href = vnd.unilang:ham.html>ham</a> as the final prize.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hamvraag.html>hamvraag</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hamvraag.html>hamvragen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hamvraag.html>hamvraagje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>million-dollar question <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">the final, critical or most important question, the crux</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><b>2004</b>, Yvonne Keuls, <i>Familiegedoe</i>, Ambo.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl">‘<a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hamvraag.html>hamvraag</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:natuurlijk.html>natuurlijk</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gevaarlijk.html>gevaarlijk</a>?’ poneert <a href = vnd.unilang:meneer.html>meneer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mercedes.html>Mercedes</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">"Of course the <b>million-dollar question</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> he dangerous?" states <a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:mercedes.html>Mercedes</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:handelen.html>handelen</a> (2951)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:handelen.html>handelen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">handalon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*handlōną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">hand</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-elen</i>.
</p>
